## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[fetchWatchedTotes()] --> B[dispatch REQUEST_WATCHED_TOTES]
    B --> C[dispatch REQUEST_WATCHED_TOTES_COUNT]
    C --> D[getState() -> pageSize, pageNumber]
    D --> E[build url = apiUrl("/containertracking/api/watch")]
    E --> F[axios.get(url, {headers, params})]
    F -->|success| G[dispatch RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES_COUNT (totalPages)]
    G --> H[dispatch RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES (watchedTotes)]
    F -->|error| I[console.error(error)]
    I --> J[dispatch RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES_ERROR (error)]
```

> SVG rendering failed for this diagram.

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> idle
    idle : initialState\nwatchedTotesLoading=false\npageIndex=0\npageSize=10\npageCount=0
    idle --> loading : REQUEST_WATCHED_TOTES / set watchedTotesLoading=true
    loading --> loaded : RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES / watchedTotes=payload,watchedTotesLoading=false
    loading --> error : RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES_ERROR / watchedTotesLoading=false
    loading --> countUpdated : RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES_COUNT / watchedTotesPageCount=payload.totalPages
    countUpdated --> loaded : RECEIVE_WATCHED_TOTES / watchedTotes=payload,watchedTotesLoading=false
    anyState --> indexUpdated : SET_WATCHED_TOTES_PAGE_INDEX / watchedTotesPageIndex=payload.pageIndex
    loaded --> idle
    error --> idle
```
